# Workflow Routing Removal Audit

Generated from the owner-routing retirement term list after the current cleanup pass. The migration, validation SQL, and regression guard are intentionally excluded from this active-reference list because they contain retired names solely to drop/check them.

## Replacement Model

OVERWATCH for ALFA uses section/workflow routing rather than workflow routing. Findings are triaged by severity, status, evidence, and the owning dashboard workflow. Ticket/change ID and verification fields support closure where required.

- Documentation: 53
- Other active reference: 7
- Python logic: 28
- ACTIVE_VALIDATION_SQL: 908
- Test: 251
